precision highp float;
in vec2 sample_coordinate;
uniform sampler2D plane0;
uniform mat3 transform;
out vec4 frag_out;
#if BIPLANAR
uniform sampler2D plane12;
uniform sampler2D plane1;
uniform sampler2D plane2;
#endif
void main() {
#if BIPLANAR
    vec2 plane12_in = vec2(texture(plane12, sample_coordinate).xy);
    vec3 planar_in = vec3(texture(plane0, sample_coordinate).x, plane12_in.x - 0.5, plane12_in.y - 0.5);
    vec3 planar_in = vec3(
        texture(plane0, sample_coordinate).x,
        texture(plane1, sample_coordinate).x - 0.5,
        texture(plane2, sample_coordinate).x - 0.5
    );
#endif
    frag_out = vec4(transform * planar_in, 1.0);

#if CHROMA
#define OFFSET 0.5
layout(location = 1) out float plane1_out;
#define OFFSET 0.0
#endif

    plane1_out = transformed.EXTRACT_PLANE1 + OFFSET;
#endif
